<t>CREATE TABLE compliance_regulations (
  regulation_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  regulation_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE compliance_documents (
  document_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  document_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  regulation_id INT,
  FOREIGN KEY (regulation_id) REFERENCES compliance_regulations(regulation_id)
);

  issue_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  issue_description TEXT NOT NULL,
  document_id INT,
  FOREIGN KEY (document_id) REFERENCES compliance_documents(document_id)
);
